Anti-Japanese sentiment is extremely high in various parts of the Northeast, and anti-Japanese troops have sprung up everywhere. The most difficult to deal with for the Japanese are the troops of Ma Zhanshan, Wang Delin, Ding Chao, and Li Du. The people's hearts are also extremely angry, for several reasons: (1) The Japanese army harasses and rapes everywhere, and women must take off their tops to be inspected when entering and leaving the city gates. (2) Rifles are the second life of the people's militias. The Japanese ordered them to be registered, and then planned to confiscate them after registration. (3) The former Qing Dynasty Interior Ministry's Banner Land is now being forcibly recovered by the pseudo-state according to the maps, and those who own the land are immediately bankrupt. The Japanese are also using Koreans to gradually occupy the land. (4) Chinese traitors are colluding with the Japanese army to extort wealthy households and choose the fat ones to devour. Because of these reasons, everyone is in danger, so they have all risen up. In total, the anti-Japanese army has more than 2 million rifles and fights anytime and anywhere, making the Japanese army exhausted and妄想扑灭 thinking of extinguishing them. However, the so-called invasion of Pingjin before the Japanese army has extinguished the anti-Japanese forces is a propaganda effort by the other side. In fact, the Japanese army does not have time for this. The next month will be the critical moment for the success or failure of the anti-Japanese army. If the Japanese army cannot extinguish the volunteer army in this month, then the green gauze curtain will rise, and the Japanese army will be even more helpless. However, the anti-Japanese armies lack ammunition and urgently need replenishment, and they also lack unified command, which is their shortcoming. While I was in western Liaoning, the Japanese gradually paid attention to me and sent detectives to follow me. After arriving in Ping, I met with Premier Wang Jingwei and learned that there were already some solutions, but a drop in the bucket is still useless. This time I came to Nanjing to report my findings to the central government. The Japanese are now unscrupulous in the Northeast, so diplomatic tactics, no matter how good, are no longer applicable and must be resisted by force. At this time when the volunteer army is active, if the central government does not think of using them again, I am afraid that it will be too late, and they will be destroyed by the Japanese, anesthetizing their thoughts, and it will be even more difficult to recover at that time." (26th)

Banditry on the Pinghan Railway 94

Red Bandits Claiming to be the Fourth Division Attack Wusheng Pass with Main Force

Tracks Destroyed, Stations Burned, Employees Kidnapped

Hubei and Henan Send Troops to Suppress, Fierce Fighting Occurs at Lijiazhai

Hankou Dispatch, The southern section of the Pinghan Railway between Xiaogan and Guangshui has been harassed by bandits three times recently, causing passenger and freight trains to derail three times. On the morning of the 26th of this month, at 3 am, there was another bandit alarm at Lujiashan, 96 kilometers from Hankou. It was reported that a force claiming to be the Fourth Division, which attacked Guangshan and Hanchuan, intended to disrupt the Pinghan Railway. The bandits first dismantled the tracks on a small bridge north of Lujiashan, causing locomotive No. 613, which was pulling empty slag cars, to derail completely at that location. The Lujiashan station was also destroyed by the bandits, and a portion of the guard car No. 914 attached to the train was burned. Stationmaster Wang Gongchang, ticket seller Cai Pingqi, brakemen Zhang Fusheng, Liu Fa, Chen Shuwu, track worker Li, gateman Hong, flagman Yang, and patrol officer Sun, a total of eleven people, were guarded by the bandits and then kidnapped. At the same time, twelve rails were also dismantled by the bandits at the 1012-kilometer mark of Dongshuanghe, and four track workers from Section 274 were kidnapped. Electric poles between Dongshuanghe and Liulin were also cut down. The No. 12 long-distance passenger train from Hankou to Ping ceased operation immediately that day, and the No. 52 short-distance passenger train only traveled to Xiaojiagang. The long-distance passenger train from Ping to Hankou traveled to Guangshui and was changed to No. 12 and returned to Beiping. The Pinghan Railway Bureau repeatedly received reports from stations along the line and telegraphed He Chengjun, the pacification commissioner stationed in Hubei, and Wang Renliu Zhi, the pacification commissioner stationed in Henan, to request the dispatch of troops to suppress the bandits. At the same time, many technicians and workers were dispatched, carrying heavy materials, and traveling to the site under the escort of armored cars to rush the repairs, and ordered the heads of the Xinyang transportation, mechanical, and engineering sections to cooperate in the repairs. On the 27th, continued reports from various stations stated that the bandits had retreated, and five of the kidnapped employees had escaped. However, there were still many bandits hiding in the mountains near the 1010 and 1020-kilometer marks, and the main force of the bandits in the Lijiazhai area was engaged in fierce fighting with the 15th Route Army of Ma Hongkui. In addition to the 2nd and 3rd Divisions stationed in Henan, which had departed from Zhengzhou to Minggang, and Ma Hongkui's troops, which had departed for Lijiazhai, the 13th Division of Wan Yaohuang, stationed in Hubei, had first departed for Lujiashan to cover the repairs. Division Commander Wan Yaohuang went to Hankou that day to command. The 10th Division of Li Mo'an, recently arrived in Hankou, was also ordered to depart and cooperate in the suppression. According to railway bureau officials, the troop strength protecting the railway has been increased, and the damaged tracks can be repaired. Therefore, the second special express train has been allowed to pass first. The bureau had previously telegraphed the Ministry of Railways to report the incident, and the following are the two telegrams: (1) To Minister Gu, according to the telegram from the police section chief of Xinyang, the defeated bandits attacking Huangguang are now gathering the strength of the Fourth Division and dividing into two routes to harass the west, one attacking Guangshui and the other attacking Liulin. The 15th Route Army has been ordered to rush to defend, and the Xinyang station has been ordered to prepare cars to transport reinforcements. Also, the director of the Xinyang office, Zhou Xiaochao, telegraphed that the 2nd and 3rd Divisions and Chairman Liu's special train, and three regiments of special forces, were heading south and stationed in Minggang. Special report. (2) To Minister Gu, regarding the derailment of the No. 11 train yesterday, the situation this afternoon is reported further for your inspection: 1. Since last night, the main force of the bandits and Ma Hongkui's troops have been fighting fiercely near Lijiazhai. Many electric poles between Shuanghe and Liulin have been dismantled by the bandits. 2. A demolition team of about 1,000 bandits arrived at Lujiashan station on the 26th and kidnapped more than ten people, including the stationmaster. Telegraph, road signs, and tracks were all destroyed. Locomotive No. 613, carrying a train of sleepers, derailed at a small bridge north of the station. Many electric poles and sleepers were destroyed. 3. The radio report from the defense forces stated that the bridge on the Yanhe River near Weijiadian was also dismantled before dawn, causing heavy damage. Two trains of empty cars were also destroyed. 4. According to the above situation, the bandits are attacking Wusheng Pass with their main force and sending demolition teams to dismantle the roads everywhere. It is difficult to guarantee that major incidents will not occur tonight. In addition to requesting the stationed troops to protect the area and sending personnel to rush to repair the tracks for traffic, this report is hereby submitted. (June 27th)

Flooding Disaster in Jiangxi Province 95

The Gan River and Fu River Banks are a Vast Expanse of Water

Newly Constructed Dikes from Work Relief Efforts Also Collapsed in Many Places

Nanchang Correspondence: For several years, the various districts of Jiangxi Province have been ravaged by bandits. The only areas that can be considered relatively peaceful are a few counties in the lower reaches of the Gan River and near Poyang Lake in northern Jiangxi, more than ten counties near Nanchang, and Fuzhou, where transportation is relatively convenient. However, last year's floods caused more than half of the dikes in the counties along the Gan River and near Poyang Lake to collapse. Even places that had not suffered from human disasters were struck by natural disasters. The Provincial Relief Committee and the Provincial Government, together with the Central Relief Committee, organized work relief projects, recruited displaced refugees, and rushed to repair the collapsed dikes. By this spring, the collapsed dikes in Jiujiang, Poyang, Yongxiu, and Xinjian had been repaired. At the same time, seeds were distributed, and spring plowing began. The flood victims along the Gan River were hoping for a harvest to survive, but since the beginning of summer, the weather has been cold and overcast, as if it were spring. As the saying goes, "If you don't use a fan in April, you can see the early rice." Even without floods, the rice harvest would inevitably be reduced. However, since the middle of this month, the weather has changed even more, with continuous cold rain. Even in the height of summer, people are still wearing lined clothing. Those in the know had long recognized this as a sign of a coming flood. Indeed, in the past ten days, the river water has continued to rise. By the 20th, water level measurements at the Water Conservancy Bureau showed that the water level was only one meter lower than during last year's major flood. From the 23rd to the 26th, torrential rain fell day and night. The lower-lying areas of the city were flooded. The Jiaojiao Bridge area could only be crossed by vehicle. Upon inspection outside Zhangjiang Gate, the water of the Gan River had already reached the road. Across the river, a vast expanse of water could be seen. The houses of the people on the洲 (zhou, islands in the river) and along the banks were level with the water. Hundreds of acres of lush and lovely rice fields had become a boundless expanse of water, with only a few treetops visible, dotting the surface. According to reports from the Water Police Bureau, the Water Conservancy Bureau, and other sources, the Jiangfeng dike, located two li below 市 (shi, city) on the east bank of the Gan River, sixty li from the provincial capital, was in imminent danger due to the overwhelming force of the water. Engineers from the Water Conservancy Bureau and philanthropists such as Huang Wenzhi purchased a large number of sacks and wooden stakes to reinforce the dike. Nearby residents also gathered crowds, day and night, to help. However, on the 24th, the dike still collapsed for more than ten zhang (丈, traditional Chinese unit of length) in the midst of strong winds and heavy rain. The area within the dike, hundreds of li in length, immediately turned into a swamp. Residents climbed trees and roofs to survive. The rice seedlings and livestock had no chance of survival. The Fuyou and Dayou dikes, which are closely related to the provincial capital, have also been almost level with the water in recent days. According to the Water Conservancy Bureau, if the heavy rain continues, there is little chance of reinforcing them. If these two dikes collapse, the Yuzhang Ditch and the Guangrun Gate South Gate will have to be closed to prevent floodwaters from entering the provincial capital. Other districts have also reported flooding. According to boatmen from the upper reaches of the Gan River, the Jiao River in Xingguo has flooded, with the water in the county seat being more than one zhang deep. The water level in the Ji'an area is much higher than usual. According to express boat messages from the Fu River, the area along the river from Linchuan and above is a vast expanse of water. The Dabao dike in Xiefu, near the provincial capital, has only a foot or so above the water. Farmers are desperately sounding gongs to call for help. Inquiries from boats from the Yuan River and the Xiu River all reported that the river water was overflowing. The water from all of these rivers flows into the Gan River and Poyang Lake. It is said that the water level of the Yangtze River has been very high recently, with the river water flowing backward into Poyang Lake. The water of the Gan River is flowing southward, causing flooding. The newly built dikes around Jiujiang and Poyang Lake are all in danger. Residents in the vicinity, having suffered the hardship of displacement and starvation last year, are instinctively fearful and have reported the disaster to the Provincial Government and the Provincial Relief Committee, requesting funds for reinforcement. In response, Chairman Xiong has allocated several thousand yuan to the Water Conservancy Bureau for reinforcement and ordered the Public Security Bureau to investigate food supplies to prepare for famine relief. The Provincial Relief Committee has sent a telegram to the central government requesting funds and plans to organize emergency relief to help refugees who are unable to cook in the water. In terms of transportation, the floods in various districts have had a significant impact. The Dagangkou Guangfu dike area on the Gan-Guangdong Road, the Wenzhen area on the Gan-Zhejiang Road, and the Yunshan sections of the Gan-Fujian Road have all been flooded, and traffic has been suspended. It is reported that the low-lying areas of the Nanxun Railway near the Xiu River are also about to be flooded. If the weather does not clear up, the Nanxun Railway may also be forced to shut down. (27th)

Great Flood Enters Changsha 96

Areas Along the River Become a Swamp

Fortunately, Rice-Producing Areas Are Not Affected

Changsha Correspondence: For the past two weeks, it has been raining continuously, causing flash floods. As a result, the water level of the Xiang River has risen sharply, and countless houses and fields along the river have been submerged. The provincial capital of Changsha is also about to become a swamp. As of the 23rd, the water level at the Changsha Customs had risen to 31 feet 6 inches. All the river streets on the waterfront, from Liupu Street to Lingguan Ferry, Chuxiang Street, Banxiang Street, Xiaoximen River Street, Daximen River Street, Fuxingmen River Street, Caohe Street, and the Xinyao River area outside the North Gate, have become a swamp. About 20,000 to 30,000 residents from 5,000 to 6,000 households along the river have moved into the city to escape. The godowns at Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, China Merchants, Hong An, and Nissin docks are all submerged in six to seven feet of water. These shipping companies have notified merchants to quickly remove goods stored in warehouses, otherwise they will not be responsible for any damage. Poor families living along the river have nowhere to live and have moved into public temples in the city for temporary shelter. The cries of children are extremely pitiful. Commercial activities and transportation outside the city have been completely cut off. From the 23rd to the evening of the 24th, the heavy rain continued. At 4:00 PM on the 24th, the water level at the Changsha Customs was 33 feet 9 inches, which was 2 feet 3 inches higher than on the 23rd. As a result, floodwaters entered the city from the river streets. In the southern district, the water rushed in from Gutan Street and went straight to the Xuegong Gate, with the water inside the city being about a foot deep. In the western district, the water entered from the Xiaoximen and Daximen Gates and reached Luopeng Bridge, going straight up West Chang Street. In addition, Fuxingmen and Caochao Gates have also been flooded. The water on Zhongshan Road has submerged the entrance to Xiaodong Street. In the northern district, the water has reached the Martyrs' Shrine and is about to reach the city gate. However, the Tongtai Gate is located in a lower-lying area, where the water is five to six feet deep. The Mingde Middle School and Zhou Nan Girls' School inside the Tongtai Gate have been completely submerged, and classes have been suspended. Only the tops of newly planted trees along the river streets above Caochao Gate are visible. At higher points along the river streets, the water has sealed off the doors, while at lower points, the water is about to reach the rooftops. Small boats are moving along the streets, transporting people. Many houses have collapsed along the streets. Except for large ships between Xiangtan and Hankou that continue to operate as usual, all other ships have been suspended. Five to six thousand longshoremen have lost their jobs because they cannot load or unload cargo. The Dalv Middle School and Guangyi Middle School, as well as the municipal and private elementary schools at the North Gate have become underwater palaces. Teachers and students have moved into the city and cannot attend classes. Car services from Changsha to various places have been suspended. The Changtan Road has been closed due to flooding in Yijiawan. The Changheng Road cannot be opened because the water at the Xiasesi Station is six to seven feet deep. The Changbao Road has not been opened due to road damage caused by mountain floods in the Xiangtan and Xiangxiang areas. Transportation throughout the province has been greatly affected. The losses to dikes and levees along the Xiang River are even greater. The 十萬壠 (Shi Wan Long), 楊梅洲 (Yang Mei Zhou), and other places in Xiangtan County, as well as 爛泥圍 (Lan Ni Wei), 韓家湖 (Han Jia Hu), 梅溪灘 (Mei Xi Tan), 三里壠 (San Li Long), 三汶磯 (San Wen Ji), 施家港 (Shi Jia Gang), 羊湖 (Yang Hu), and other places in Changsha County, have all become swamps. Countless rice seedlings have been submerged. The entire city of Xiangtan County has also been flooded. Xiangyin, You County, Xiangyin, and Hengshan counties have also telegraphed reports of flooding. As a result, the price of rice in Changsha has soared, with the price of rice per dan (石, traditional Chinese unit of volume) rising by five jiao (角, a monetary unit) in two days. The price of vegetables has also risen by more than one-third compared to the previous few days due to the flooding of nearby vegetable gardens. As of today (the 25th), the heavy rain has not stopped, and the water level continues to rise. There is no hope for the weather to clear up in the near future. People are worried about their livelihoods. Fortunately, this flood is from the southern rivers, so the affected areas are only in the southern and central parts of Hunan. The counties around Dongting Lake, which are known for their abundant rice production, are affected by the western rivers. The water level has not risen significantly, and the dikes and levees should be safe for the time being. As long as they can hold out for half a month, the early rice can be harvested. This will not only benefit the finances and livelihoods of the people of Hunan, but also ensure that there will be no shortage of food for the people in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. If the weather does not clear up and the southern rivers affect the western rivers, the future will be unthinkable. (June 25th)

Dangerous Condition of the Grand Canal Project 97

Without 500,000 in Relief Funds

The Project Will Inevitably Fall Short

The Jiangbei Canal is the general hub for the downstream waters of Shandong, Anhui, and Henan provinces. It relies entirely on the east and west dikes for protection. Last year, the Gao Shao breach caused more than twenty breaches, with a total length of nine hundred zhang. The fields, houses, and property of the counties east of the dikes suffered losses of over 300 million, and countless lives were lost. It can be described as an unprecedented catastrophe. The breaching and dike restoration project initially faced difficult fundraising and repeated delays. Until Han Guojun, as a respected elder from his hometown, took on the difficult task and established an office in Yangzhou. The entire construction cost was reduced as much as possible. In addition to the preliminary expenditure of nearly 400,000 yuan by the provincial government for the breaching project, there was still a net need for more than 3.6 million yuan. In recent months, thanks to the Water Disaster Relief Committee, the US Wheat Relief Program, and the funds allocated by various parties in the provincial government, as well as the subsidies from the Chinese and Foreign Relief Association, eight-tenths of the entire project has been completed despite all the difficulties. Farmers in various counties are eating Guanyin clay and engaging in agricultural work, hoping for a good autumn harvest to extend this lifeline. However, recently the construction funds have been exhausted, and there is still a shortfall of over 500,000 yuan, leading to concerns that the project will fall short. Earthwork accounts for four-tenths of the unfinished sections, especially the materials needed for each section, such as lining, crushed stone, and accumulated soil, which are the most important. The water level is rising rapidly, and the opportunity to rush the transport is urgent and cannot be delayed. Han Guojun went to the province to request funds. The provincial government, facing a financial crisis, was unable to respond. It is reported that they have jointly requested the National Government Water Disaster Relief Committee to allocate funds from the central relief fund in accordance with the amount needed, in order to overcome this difficulty. It is uncertain whether the association can provide as much assistance as possible, so that the entire canal project will not fail before completion and suffer another catastrophe.

Qingdao Citizens Oppose Japanese Merchants Contracting for Pier No. 5 of the Grand Port 98

Rumors Spread That a Contract Has Been Signed with Japanese Merchants

Government Officials Have Not Formally Announced It

Qingdao Correspondence: The construction of Pier No. 5 of the Grand Port in Qingdao is a matter of great importance to the prosperity and decline of Qingdao City. Since the city government proposed the construction, citizens and various organizations have been happy to cooperate with the city government to discuss raising construction funds, hoping to see the project completed as soon as possible. The Chamber of Commerce has been particularly active and has organized a fund management committee to carefully plan. In the previous bidding process, the Japanese-owned Fuchang Company won the bid with a price of 3.9 million yuan. Citizens opposed it, and public opinion was outraged, demanding that the authorities revoke Fuchang's construction qualifications. Recently, Japanese newspapers in Qingdao suddenly reported that the mayor and Chuanbian, the representative of Fuchang, had signed a contract at the city government at 6:30 PM on the 18th. However, inquiries from various parties to the city government and the fund management committee have been vague, without any formal or reliable statement. The situation is deeply suspicious. The details of the process are explored and recorded below.

The Motivation for Constructing Pier No. 5: Pier No. 5 of the Grand Port is the key to the prosperity of Qingdao's commerce. Because it is deep enough to accommodate large ocean liners, they can dock and unload cargo, which is extremely convenient. The project is also huge, with a total construction cost of 4 million yuan. Although the city government has drafted a construction plan, the pier fund management committee only has 600,000 to 700,000 yuan, which is far from the total amount. Therefore, it was decided to use a method of paying in installments, with the construction period set at four years. After the commencement of construction, payments would be made every four months, in twelve installments. This amount can be accumulated gradually within four years. To establish the fund and maintain credit, the city government and various organizations jointly formed a fund management committee to demonstrate cooperation between officials and the people.

The Process of Advertising and Bidding: After the construction plan was drafted, the city government advertised for contractors in Beijing, Shanghai, and other places. Many merchants from China, Germany, Denmark, and Japan submitted bids. For the sake of prudence, the city government formed a procurement committee to review the qualifications of each bidder and decided to award the contract to the lowest bidder.

Page 9

Important News

As a result, the bids were: 孤山 (Gu Shan), a Japanese merchant, 2.7 million yuan; Fuchang Company, a Japanese merchant, 3.9 million yuan; Kangyi 洋行 (Yanghang, foreign firm), a joint venture between Chinese, German, and Danish interests, 3.95 million yuan; Okura Corporation, a Japanese merchant, 4.15 million yuan; Fuji Construction Company, a Chinese merchant, 4.445 million yuan; and Sinli 洋行, a German merchant, 4.875777 million yuan. However, 孤山 (Gu Shan) of the Japanese merchant attached a condition to the bid, requiring the city government to pay 700,000 yuan in advance when signing the contract and not using Qixin 馬牌 (Ma Pai, Horse Brand) cement in accordance with the regulations, so it was rejected by the procurement committee. Therefore, the lowest bidder was Fuchang Company of the Japanese merchant. After review by the procurement committee, it was submitted to the mayor for approval, and Fuchang Company was awarded the contract.

Reasons for Citizen Opposition: It is found that the Japanese merchant Fuchang Company is located in Dalian, and only a representative is stationed in Qingdao. Last year, when bidding for the construction of Qingdao's Qianhai pier, they won the bid with the lowest price of around 230,000 yuan. After promotion by the Japanese Consul and others, the contract was about to be signed, but they intended to change the drawings and regulations, so they bribed a key member of the Qingdao City Government with a large sum of money, intending to seek protection. Unexpectedly, the official presented the赃物 (zangwu, bribe) to the city government, and Mayor Hu Ruoyu was furious and immediately revoked their qualifications, and the German Sinli 洋行, whose bid was about 40,000 yuan higher, was substituted. The Japanese Consul was also unable to help. This time, the procurement committee failed to investigate and awarded such a large project to them, which caused citizens to have deep doubts. Therefore, several representatives were sent to the city government to petition, state the advantages and disadvantages, and demand the cancellation of their contract. As for the lowest bidder besides 孤山 (Gu Shan) Kiln, it was not Fuchang Company, but Kangyi 洋行, a joint venture between Chinese, German, and Danish interests, because the bid of 3.95 million yuan of this company included the excavation cost of 60,000 yuan for submarine rocks. The actual bid was only 3.89 million yuan, which was still 10,000 yuan lower than that of the Japanese merchant Fuchang Company. The submarine rock layers at the construction site of Pier No. 5 are uneven. Some places are as low as several feet, all of which are silt. If they are not excavated and filled with cement foundations, the pier foundation will not be firm. This is completely an engineering problem. Because this point was not considered in the city government's plan, the engineer of Kangyi 洋行, a Dane, who has rich experience in pier construction, specially explained this point, so he added a clause in the bid, calculating the engineering cost of 60,000 yuan. This amount was not included by other bidders, but it was actually necessary to include it. However, the city government and the procurement committee disregarded the importance of the project and the expectations of the people and rashly announced that Fuchang won the bid, no wonder the citizens rose up in opposition.

Rumors of Both Parties Signing the Contract: The Qingdao City Government notified the Japanese merchant Fuchang Company on May 16 this year, after the bidding was opened, that it should provide a guarantee (must be a wealthy Chinese merchant) and sign the contract within one week in accordance with the bidding regulations. However, in the face of the current national crisis, the unresolved Northeast issue, and the Japanese arson attack on the city party headquarters, etc., these events are still lingering in the minds of citizens. Therefore, Fuchang, in addition to finding Mitsubishi 洋行 as a guarantor, had no possibility of finding another wealthy Chinese merchant as a guarantor in accordance with the regulations. For this reason, the signing of the contract has been delayed for a month. However, the Japanese are cunning and scheming. On the 22nd, a Japanese newspaper in Qingdao announced that both parties had signed the contract and would start construction soon, and claimed that Mayor Shen Honglie had formally signed the contract with Mr. Chuanbian, the representative of Fuchang, at the city government at 6:30 PM on the 18th. However, inquiries from various parties to the city government and the procurement committee have not been able to confirm this. Such a huge project, the signing of the contract is of course very important, and there is no case where it has been signed without being formally announced. It is inevitable that the Japanese are using treacherous tactics to probe social opinion and to further promote the Japanese merchants. Now that the citizens of Qingdao are firmly opposed to Fuchang Company undertaking the construction, the mayor should pay close attention to this matter.

Major Fire in Songjiang West Gate 99

Songjiang West Gate Street is the most prosperous commercial area. Less than ten days after the robbery of the Chinese Industrial Bank at Yue Miao Kou, Dafeng Silk Store and other neighboring stores opposite were struck by fire, and many neighboring stores were burned. The intensity of the fire was rarely seen in recent times. The fire started at 12:30 PM today (28th) on the upper floor of Dafeng, when a gasoline lamp was being tested. It was said that the shop owner had a happy event and was going to use the lamp for lighting. The apprentice Cao Xiaoliang, who was only fourteen years old and was testing the lamp, accidentally caused the gasoline bottle to explode with a loud bang. The shop assistants downstairs and the neighbors on the left and right suspected it was a bomb. Then they saw the apprentice covered in fire running downstairs. He stumbled and fell in the center of the shop, rolling around on the ground. The shop assistants knew that a disaster had occurred and quickly used cloth to put out the fire on his body. Unexpectedly, the cloth also caught fire, and more than ten pieces were used. Not only was the staircase burned, but the shop was filled with smoke and flames, making it impossible to approach. The police on duty blew the whistle to warn, and soon pumps from various places rushed to the scene. Dafeng had already burst through the roof, spreading to Tang Sanju Shoe Store on the left and several stores on the opposite side, including a meat store, a candy store, and a pipe store. The Chinese Industrial Bank was spared because of its high and thick walls. The county magistrate, district chief, public security bureau chief, regimental commander of the garrison, and land and water police all arrived to suppress the situation. Cai Zhongyu, the president of the fire brigade, ran back and forth, directing each team with great effort. The military and police stood guard to maintain traffic. When the fire at Dafeng first started, there was a visitor wearing a Zhongshan suit who broke in and snatched three pieces of Zhongshan ge cloth before trying to escape. He was arrested by the police and identified himself as Li Feipeng from Hunan. He was immediately handed over to the Public Security Bureau and then to the court for interrogation. For a time, all the shops on the street closed their doors and took strict precautions. By 2:00 PM, the fire had weakened slightly. The kitchen at the rear of Dafeng, which was connected by a cement bridge, was also affected. Therefore, at the height of the fire, flames erupted on all four sides, left, right, front, and back. Fortunately, the fire brigade members were brave and enthusiastic, and Yang Shijie, the inspector of the Public Security Bureau, and his entire team of detectives also helped with the extinguishing, preventing the fire from spreading. However, neighboring stores such as Changshun Restaurant and Zhengda Silk Shop suffered minor damage to their storefronts and roofs. By 2:30 PM, the fire was extinguished, but embers remained, making a rekindling possible. Some pumps were left at the Yue Temple and other locations to prepare for any further firefighting. After the investigation, the apprentice who was injured was the son of the owner of the Hu Tong Silk Thread Store. The family was extremely saddened upon hearing the news. Dafeng Silk Shop was completely destroyed except for the account books that were taken out. Tang Sanju Shoe Store had no time to take anything away. The total losses from this incident amounted to more than 100,000 yuan, a true catastrophe.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 100

Meeting of the Defense Committee: The county defense committee has been established and is officially in operation. Wu Dingchang from the Provincial Committee is the director of the office. A meeting of the defense committees of various districts was convened today (28th), presided over by the county magistrate and committee chairman, to discuss the funding for the defense committee. It was generally agreed that when former County Magistrate Jin was planning to establish a police brigade, he proposed to collect household registration donations based on the amount of household property, dividing them into different levels to collect donations for the police brigade. However, this was not implemented. Now that the defense committee is in urgent need of funds, it was decided to re-propose the old plan and submit the household registration donation plan of former County Magistrate Jin to the Department of Civil Affairs for approval and implementation. The issue of operating expenses for district branches was also decided to be temporarily borrowed from the respective district offices and repaid when the household registration donations are collected in the future.

Taicang 101

Misunderstanding Caused by Disinfecting Wells: The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, in view of the inevitable outbreaks of epidemics after the war, sent special personnel to the affected areas to provide free epidemic prevention injections to the people. On the 24th of this month, the Mu'ertang Boy Scouts first came from Jia to Tai and contacted the county government. Then they posted slogans along the way and informed households that they could disinfect their wells with medicine, which caused misunderstandings among the people. For a time, rumors spread among the streets. Upon hearing this, the county government immediately issued a notice to dispel doubts, and the Boy Scouts gave oral propaganda at key intersections. The doctors have already come from Jia to Tai yesterday and set up their office at the Education Bureau. Injections are scheduled to begin on the 27th.

Fengxian 102

Dishonest Merchants Privately Import Inferior Goods: A certain large merchant in Nanqiao recently entrusted a certain clothing merchant in Songjiang to purchase a large batch of inferior goods in Shanghai, worth as much as ten thousand taels of silver. In order to avoid being detected on the way, the goods were packed into clothing packages and secretly transported to Nanqiao on a Wuxi express boat the day before yesterday, where the persons in charge were changed in an attempt to mix the goods and sell them. All circles in this county were angered by the fact that this dishonest merchant had been privately transporting inferior goods more than once. Yesterday afternoon, the various trade associations reported this to the local National Salvation Association in writing and convened an emergency meeting. As a result of the discussion, it was determined that the matter was of great importance. In addition to sending a letter of warning from the association, it was also learned that the inferior goods imported by the store this time were mostly fabrics with the brands of Double Child, Flying Fish, Four Gentlemen, and Yang Crane. The trademarks, as well as the fabric patterns, were drawn and displayed on the thoroughfare for people to identify and avoid being deceived.

Suzhou 103

Death of Mr. Xu Jianqing: Mr. Xu Jianqing, a gentleman of this county, was always enthusiastic about local public welfare. Last year, he served as the manager of the Sulian Land Bank. When the Japanese invaded Shanghai, the financial situation in Suzhou was quite panicked. It was thanks to Mr. Xu's efforts that the situation was maintained. Recently, he died of illness. The funeral was held yesterday (26th) with white horses and plain carriages, which moved many people.

Changzhou 104

Major Murder Case: Jiang Jufa's adopted son Jiang Tianzhen from the fifth district of Wu County, two or three li from Dongqing Town, was secretly murdered by his wife and his uncle and 田夥 (tianhuo, field laborer) due to their adultery. His body was cut into three sections and moved to a mulberry field near Xuejiatou Village in Cheng County for burial. Recently, Yang Kongyi, the chief prosecutor of the county court, heard about this and reported it. Secret agents were dispatched to investigate and confirmed the facts. Then, detectives from the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau took measures to arrest the key suspect Wang Fada, who confessed to the crime during preliminary interrogation. He was escorted to the city for interrogation yesterday (27th).

County Budget Deficit of 50,000 Yuan: The Wu County government convened a county budget meeting on the 27th. At that time, after comparing various items of income and expenditure, there was a deficit of more than 50,000 yuan. After much deliberation, there were few ways to make up for the deficit. It was decided to submit the entire case for review and appoint Lu Yongchuan and eight others as reviewers to convene a review meeting first to discuss solutions.

Jiangyin 105

Rejection of Jiang Hong's Fraud Appeal: The case of Jiang Hong, former director of the relief institution, being accused by Ji Sha for fraudulent acquisition of property in the 19th year of the Republic, was judged by the county to be a fine of two hundred yuan and the return of twenty yuan to Ji Sha. Jiang refused to accept this and appealed to the Wu County District Court, which upheld the original verdict. Jiang again refused to accept it and appealed to the High Court, which sent it back to the District Court for retrial, sentencing Jiang to a fine of one hundred yuan and the return of twenty yuan to Ji Sha. Jiang still refused to accept this and appealed to the High Court again. Cao Yuanmo, the director of the relief institution, also participated, presenting to the High Court that Ji Sha's twenty yuan was donated to the institution, and the court's decision to return it was unfair. Zhang Yipeng was hired as a lawyer for defense. The District Court Prosecutor Lu Wenqin also presented a defense, stating that the grounds for appeal were solely based on the argument that the two thousand yuan from Ji Sha was donated to the relief institution, denying any intention of fraud. However, it was found that Ji Sha's payment was made when her son was detained by the county government on suspicion of being a communist. Her purpose was for the defendant to find a way to rescue her son from prison, which Ji Sha had testified to in detail. Ji Sha and the defendant had no prior animosity, so her words were credible. The defendant, serving in public office and being a party member, should have known that judicial cases cannot be influenced by money. Yet, he deposited the money under his own name. His fraudulent acquisition of property under false pretenses was very obvious. The original judgment was appropriate. All grounds for appeal were without merit and should be rejected according to the law.

County Party Department Seals "Ke Bao" Newspaper Office: The County Party Department recently received a petition from Wang Xianzhao and 126 other citizens from Beiwai, accusing "Ke Bao" of extortion under false pretenses and endangering the life of Jiang Benli. They requested the county to severely punish and close the newspaper office. Additionally, Ren Yulin and 194 other farmers from Qingyang Township submitted a petition stating that "Ke Bao" fabricated facts, falsely accusing Gui Nü Wang Yaliang of causing a death, requesting the county to order the police to close the newspaper office and punish the editor to redress the grievance. Furthermore, Wang Tixin and other neighbors of the victim Wang Yaliang submitted a petition stating that "Ke Bao" published false news, violating the publishing law, and causing a death. After receiving the petitions, the County Executive Committee, after its 53rd committee meeting, decided to send a letter to the County Government, ordering the Public Security Bureau to send Inspector Zhao Yuting to the Zhongjie Gongci at 3 PM yesterday (the 27th) to seal the editorial department.

Zhenjiang 106

Tragic Incident of Military Ship Sinking Civilian Boat: Yesterday afternoon around 1 PM, a fishing boat was leaving Dantu Harbor and traveling on the Jiang River near Jiao Mountain's tail when it was suddenly struck from behind by a Haiqing military ship, splitting the boat in two. Six people, men, women, and children, were swept away by the waves and drowned. Fortunately, the Jiao Mountain Lifesaving Boat No. 7 heard the cries for help and rushed to rescue four people, men and women. They were rescued barely alive and were revived after emergency treatment. The boat owner's two sons, aged twelve and ten, were missing, their whereabouts unknown.

Yangzhou 107

County Police Team's Successful Suppression of Bandits: County Magistrate Yang Zirong dispatched the second police squadron leader Yang Juansheng, along with squad leaders Cheng Gongxing, Na Yanlan, and Wang Zhuxiang, leading over a hundred officers to the Guocun area in the eastern township on the evening of the 25th. They joined forces with the Taixian police team to suppress fierce bandits. They returned to the city on the afternoon of the 27th. This operation resulted in the beheading of three bandit leaders, the capture of eighteen bandits, including men and women, and suspects, two box cannons, one rifle, six homemade guns, and the rescue of six hostages (who were taken back by the Taixian police team). It was reported that three police officers were injured: Lu Guangsheng, Xu Shilian, and detective Zhang Mingkui. Lu's injury was severe, a bullet piercing his abdomen. He was transported to the city for treatment at 8 PM on the 26th and died around 10 PM. Xu was injured in the face, and Zhang was injured in the foot, neither injury being fatal.

Nantong 108

Tonghaiqi Joint Defense Against Bandits: Within the borders of Nantong, Haimen, and Qidong counties, bandits were plotting riots. The military and police discovered this through investigation and took precautions. Key criminals were captured in Qidong and are currently under interrogation. The county magistrates of the three counties, concerned about the unrest caused by the bandits, specifically consulted on joint defense and bandit suppression methods to maintain public order.

Execution of Bandit Leader from Yancheng: Xu Buming, a bandit leader from Yancheng, fled to Nantong. He was captured by the provincial guerrilla team, interrogated, and executed by firing squad.

Reduction in the Amount of Subsidy Borrowed by Liang's Troops: Liang Guanying previously sent Zhu Guoheng to Nantong to borrow 100,000 yuan from the Chamber of Commerce for military subsidies. Later, due to the inability of various industries to raise enough funds, they telegraphed Liang to request a reduction in the amount. Liang has now agreed to reduce it to 60,000 yuan.

Rugao 109

Selection of County Executive and Supervisory Committee Members: The candidates for the Executive and Supervisory Committees of this county have been selected by the Provincial Party Department. The names are as follows: Executive Committee members: Wang Taikui, Zhang Qichen, Miao Yingzhong, Lu Peixian, Huang Xitao. Alternate Executive Committee members: Yu Shizhong, Shen Yong, Tang Qiu. Supervisory Committee members: Luo Yimin, Chen Guozhen, Zhang Naicha. Alternate Supervisory Committee member: Ji Zhanbei.

Water Obstruction for Rice Planting Leads to Homicide: In the Xu Family Lane in the Dingyan District of Rugao County, Xu Junping and his sister-in-law, Xu Cao, had a dispute over water obstruction for rice planting. Xu Cao went to Xu Junping's house on the morning of the 22nd of this month and slashed his throat with a razor. Xu reported this to the Dingyan Public Security Sub-bureau and requested the county to conduct an examination. However, the bureau only transported the injured person to the county yesterday (the 25th). She died just as they arrived at the entrance of the County Public Security Bureau. The body was then taken to the ash field outside the East Gate. The County Government sent Chen, a trial officer, accompanied by Zhang, an examination official, to conduct an examination.

Education and Construction Bureaus Implement Retrenchment: The County Education Bureau, in accordance with the Provincial Department's order, implemented retrenchment, abolishing the position of section chief and only establishing seven bureau staff members. The Construction Bureau will also merge affiliated agencies such as the Public Works Department and the Water Conservancy Office, and abolish the position of section chief. Both measures will be implemented starting from July 1st.

Hangzhou 110

Raising Funds to Build a Water Diversion Dam: Due to continuous heavy rain, the water level of the Qiantang River rose rapidly, and the sand dunes on the northern bank were eroded for tens of zhang. The stone dikes along the river were in imminent danger due to the rising water. Workers had been hired to collect silk cocoon bags for emergency repairs. Although the weather cleared up yesterday, the water level had not yet receded. The river water level at the dike entrance, which was only a zhang deep during last year's flood, was measured by the Water Conservancy Bureau and found to be three zhang deep, making the situation much more dangerous than in previous years. Hangzhou Mayor Zhao Zhiyou inspected the area with the Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau yesterday and sent over seventy city government officials to supervise the workers and intensify the defenses. He also went to the Construction Department to discuss relief measures with Zeng Yangfu. It was decided to build three additional water diversion dams. The largest one would require 60,000 yuan, and the other two would require 20,000 yuan each. Repairs to the stone dikes would also be needed, with the total estimated cost being 100,000 yuan. Besides allocating 30,000 yuan from the special war donation from property rentals, the remaining 70,000 yuan would be borrowed from the banking industry, using the 8 jiao per mu tax on the 100,000 mu of sand dunes on the northern bank as collateral. Construction has already begun today.

Letter

Letter from the Huainan Xiang-E-Xi-Wan Four-Shore Transportation and Merchant Guild: 111

To the esteemed Editor of the Shen Bao:

Greetings. I recently read in your newspaper's Nanjing dispatch on June 23rd that Liang Guanying's troops, due to financial difficulties, borrowed 100,000 yuan from the Yangzhou Huai Merchants Four-Shore Guild. The Guild accused Liang of extortion and filed a complaint with the Military Affairs Commission, requesting a thorough investigation. The Military Affairs Commission forwarded it to the Ministry of Military Administration for reply. The Ministry has now telegraphed Liang, instructing him to submit a report on the matter so that it can be verified and resolved. Upon reading this, we were very surprised. The 25th Route Army Headquarters, due to a shortage of funds, had indeed sent representatives to Yangzhou and sent a letter to Chairman Wang of the Jiangdu County Chamber of Commerce, requesting him to contact the Huainan Salt Transportation Association to prepare 100,000 yuan in military funds. The merchants originally lacked the capacity, but considering the importance of military needs and local security, they reluctantly agreed to seek loans from banks and money shops and pay them in installments. They also reported the loan details to the salt affairs authorities for record, requesting that the loan be offset against salt taxes to avoid losses. This did happen, but the report that they filed a complaint with the Military Affairs Commission is completely false. Your newspaper's report is inaccurate. We are writing specifically to request a correction to avoid misunderstanding. We would be extremely grateful. Sincerely, The Huainan Xiang-E-Xi-Wan Four-Shore Transportation and Merchant Guild.

Key Education News

National Central University Students Petition, President Wang Responds with Conditions 112

Ren Hongjun Resigns as President of National Central University. On the 27th, National Central University suspended classes for a day. Starting at 8:00 AM, a general student meeting was held in the school's gymnasium, attended by over 700 students. Jiang Jiong, Yu Jizhong, and Yang Deqiao served as chairmen, and Du Zhongwen and Han Pei recorded the minutes. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Request the Executive Yuan to promptly approve Liu Guanghua's resignation as acting president and explicitly order the Dean of Academic Affairs to serve as acting president. (2) In the name of the general assembly, send letters to professors Liu Yunchou, Yang Gongda, Ji Renhao, and Fang Guangqi, asking them to immediately leave the school to apologize to the students. (3) Request the government to thoroughly investigate the corruption of disaster relief donations at National Central University and request the Control Yuan to file an indictment. (4) In the name of the general assembly, send a letter to the former president, Zhu Jiaju, requesting him to return the misappropriated disaster relief donations to the accounting department within three days and promptly remit them to disaster relief agencies. (5) Regarding the selection of the new president, the results of the previous general assembly election should be maintained. (6) Before the new president takes office, please ask the Dean of Academic Affairs to act on his behalf. (7) In the name of the general assembly, warn Zhu Jiaju. (8) In the name of the general assembly, send a telegram nationwide opposing Zhu Jiaju as Minister of Education and request the Executive Yuan to dismiss Zhu Jiaju. (9) Regarding the issues of the president and funding, the Funding Standing Committee and the Student Union will be fully responsible for handling them. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. Afterwards, all the students, led by Yu Jizhong and others, went to the Executive Yuan to petition. When they passed the Ministry of Education gate, they were fortunately stopped by a student-organized disciplinary team, which advised them not to rush in and to discuss the matter after reaching the Executive Yuan. All the students then marched along the street, shouting slogans such as "Down with Zhu Jiaju!" and "Support the financial independence of National Central University!" and went directly to the Executive Yuan to petition. At 12:10 PM, as they arrived near the Executive Yuan, President Wang happened to arrive in a car and was immediately surrounded. They strongly requested him to get out of the car. After Wang's polite explanation and agreement to meet them in the auditorium of the Executive Yuan, they swarmed into the building, surrounding him both in front and behind. Ten minutes later, Wang instructed the petitioners to appoint three representatives to report the details of their requests in detail. He would then reply to them in the auditorium. He stated that regarding their requests: (1) To approve Liu Guanghua's resignation and explicitly order the Dean of Academic Affairs to serve as acting president: Wang said that although Acting President Liu had left the school, his letter of resignation had not yet arrived at the Executive Yuan, so it was inconvenient to send another person to act on his behalf. If Liu's resignation letter was already at the Ministry of Education, then it could be resolved at tomorrow's Executive Yuan meeting. (2) Due to the regulations on the exchange of notes for Sino-British Boxer Indemnity funds, it was not convenient to allocate Boxer Indemnity interest as a guarantee for National Central University's funding. He would need to investigate and reply later. (3) The dismissal of Minister of Education Zhu Jiaju involved the entire administrative situation of the Executive Yuan, so it was inconvenient to reply at this time. Regarding points (1) and (2), representatives could be appointed to come to the Executive Yuan to listen to the results of the meeting. Then, Vice Minister of Education Duan Xipeng replied, stating that regarding the president issue, Mr. Ren had agreed to come to Nanjing within the next few days. If Mr. Ren did not come, one of the three people you designated would be appointed to take the position. Mr. Zhu Kezhen had been telegraphed several times, and I had also discussed it with him in person. If President Ren firmly resigned, he could come to Nanjing. When reporters arrived at the Ministry of Education in the afternoon, they learned that Ren Hongjun had telegraphed that day, saying that due to illness, he could not handle the heavy workload and requested approval for his resignation from National Central University, and to appoint another capable person to succeed him.

The Ministry of Education Promulgates Short-Term Primary School Curriculum Standards 117

The Ministry of Education stipulates that provinces and cities shall implement one-year short-term compulsory education starting from the 21st academic year, specifically for educating out-of-school children aged ten to sixteen. The implementation methods have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, the Ministry of Education formulated "Curriculum Standards for Short-Term Primary Schools or Short-Term Primary School Classes," which were printed and distributed to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to instruct schools to follow the curriculum standards and compile teaching materials. As for the textbooks for short-term primary schools, the Ministry of Education has invited four primary school experts to begin compiling them immediately and complete them within a month, after which they will be distributed by the Ministry to various provinces and cities for printing. The curriculum standards are listed below in installments:

Curriculum Standards for Short-Term Primary Schools or Short-Term Primary School Classes 118

I. Explanation

(1) This curriculum uses the national language as the foundation and includes the most common knowledge for citizens. (2) This curriculum is specifically for educating out-of-school children aged ten to sixteen for one year.

II. Objectives

(1) To guide the practice of inherent morality, cultivate self-respect and self-confidence in citizens, in order to restore the national spirit. (2) To enable them to know the general situation of modern domestic and foreign affairs and the trend of the world, focusing on the use of the four powers. (3) To enhance the ability of production, distribution, and calculation in daily life, and cultivate the concept of people's livelihood. (4) To recognize 1,600 characters and be able to read simple vernacular texts compiled with 1,600 characters. (5) To practice writing vernacular texts such as letters and diaries. (6) To use phonetic symbols to assist in reading simple vernacular texts.

III. Weekly Time Allocation

(1) Reading: 540 minutes (2) Composition: 60 minutes (3) Writing: 30 minutes (4) Arithmetic: 90 minutes

(1) Regarding moral education: A. Enlightenment: (1) The entire textbook is centered on restoring inherent morality. (2) Courses such as civics, history, and hygiene use honor, disgrace, prosperity, decline, strength, and weakness to explain the necessity of inherent morality. (3) Courses such as geography and nature also attribute the power of human groups to overcoming the workings of nature to inherent morality. (4) The arithmetic course uses precision, accuracy, balance, and order to guide towards moral education. B. Demonstration: (1) Use facts to prove theories. (2) Limit the use of foreigners to those with national, civil rights, or people's livelihood ideas. (3) Strive to use modern figures and facts, and gradually trace back to ancient times only when necessary.

IV. Course Content

(2) Regarding writing: A. Reading: (1) The entire textbook is arranged with history, geography, civics, nature, hygiene, etc., in equal distribution. No fairy tales, myths, or fables are used. (2) Reading of daily practical texts such as short notes, letters, and diaries. (3) Reading of simple explanatory and narrative texts. (4) Practice in checking dictionaries. (5) Recognition of commonly used punctuation marks. (6) Recognition and application of phonetic symbols. B. Composition: (1) Practice writing practical texts such as short notes and letters. (2) Application of common punctuation marks. C. Writing: (1) Writing practice of all the characters learned. (2) Writing practice of practical texts. (3) Recognition of the most commonly used cursive script in daily life. (4) Recognition of simplified and broken characters.

(3) Regarding knowledge: A. History

(1) Famous people's good words and deeds to promote the spirit of sacrifice and service. (2) Great achievements of past dynasties to revive national confidence and self-respect. (3) The reasons for the governance and chaos of past dynasties, using the emphasis on people's livelihood or lack thereof as evidence. (4) The deeds of the Premier and the martyrs, focusing on the deeds of Mr. Sun Yat-sen to be influenced by his personality. (5) Commemorative days and holidays, focusing on the cause and effect of the revolution, the history of national humiliation, and the origin of unequal treaties to arouse national patriotism.

B. Geography

(1) The general situation of China's terrain, climate, products, transportation, and regions, focusing on China's unique endowments and the Premier's construction plan to inspire ideas of benefiting the country and loving the people. (2) China's capital and important cities, focusing on the comparison between urban and rural areas to make people aware of the necessity of rural construction. (3) Each ceded territory, concession, trading port, foreign mail ship, inland navigation route, joint railway, railway loan agreement, railway, focusing on the origin of foreign insults to slightly understand the meaning of how to save the country and wash away humiliation. (4) The shape of the earth, the oceans, the continents, and the location of China and important countries in the world, focusing on the relationship between various countries and China to make people know the responsibilities that China bears internationally.

C. Civics

(1) Regarding family life: focus on love, independence, and self-reliance, and avoid selfishness and dependence. (2) Regarding social life: focus on loyalty, trustworthiness, mutual assistance, and avoid fraud and usurpation. (3) Regarding the initial stages of civil rights: focus on advocating justice (during discussion) and obeying the majority (after a decision), and avoid silence, echoing, holding dissenting opinions, and licentiousness. (4) Regarding the use of the four powers: focus on fairness and prudence, and avoid partiality and recklessness. (5) Regarding local autonomy: focus on gradual and practical steps, and avoid broad generalizations and perfunctory actions. (6) Regarding the country and foreign affairs: focus on self-improvement, equality, and avoid complacency and aggression.

D. Nature

(1) The changes in the four seasons' climate and the relationship with living things. (2) Clouds, rain, frost, dew, ice, snow, hail, wind, wind direction, temperature, humidity, etc. (3) The function of lightning and methods of avoiding lightning. (4) The causes of solar eclipses, lunar eclipses, rainbows, solar and lunar halos, meteors, comets, earthquakes, volcanoes, etc., and the elimination of superstitions. (5) The harm of mosquitoes, flies, etc., and methods of repelling them. (6) The relationship between beneficial insects, harmful insects, and crops. (7) Explanation of daily necessities such as clothing, food, housing, and transportation. (8) The promotion of cultivation, with special emphasis on afforestation. (9) Explanation of major agricultural products. (10) Prevention of floods and droughts.

E. Hygiene

(1) The structure and hygiene of the external form of the human body. (2) The structure and hygiene of the internal organs of the human body. (3) The harm of addictive products such as tobacco and alcohol. (4) Prevention of infectious diseases. (5) Public health. (6) Hygiene stories.

F. Arithmetic (Mixed teaching of written calculation and abacus calculation)

(1) The recognition of teachings and the writing of teaching words. (2) Addition and subtraction. (3) Multiplication table, division song. (4) Multiplication with factors of one to three digits. (5) Division with factors of one to two digits. (6) Application of four operations. (7) Four operations with decimals. (8) Conversion of jin and liang to foreign weights and measures and currency. (9) Discounts and interest. (10) Methods of bookkeeping and accounting.

Ma Xiangbo's original letters to President Wang of the Executive Yuan, Minister of Education Zhu, President Yu of the Control Yuan, and President Jiao of the Legislative Yuan are as follows: To the esteemed President Wang, in the face of national crisis, it is necessary to focus on agriculture and industry for long-term resistance, which I believe Your Excellency also agrees with. The National Labor University has made a unique contribution to the promotion and improvement of agricultural and industrial labor culture over the years, which is an undeniable responsibility for the country and society to initiate and preserve. Although it has been devastated by the violent Japanese, recovery is still easy. However, the disposition of closing it is unbearable for general public opinion. Now, the teachers and students of the Nursing School, with the enthusiasm of patriotism, earnestly request to uphold justice and leave a glimmer of hope for agricultural and industrial education, which is vital to the life of the country. I humbly petition on their behalf, hoping for your care to comfort the eager expectations of the people. The future of the country truly depends on it. I respectfully wish you peace, Ma Xiangbo Liangqi, June 28th. Ma Xiaoche Wins the China Youth Handball Championship 124

Defeats Cao Weilin in the Final 2-0 Yesterday at 5 PM, Cao Weilin and Ma Xiaoche played a public singles handball final in the China Youth Basketball Hall, which was packed with spectators. The match was started by referee Hong Yukui. After two hours of bloody battle, Ma Xiaoche emerged as the final victor. The two games are summarized as follows:

Game 1 Cao Weilin served first. The two sides competed point by point, from 1-1 to 2-2 to 3-3 to 4-4, alternating leads until 12 points. Then, Old Ma roared and scored six consecutive points, taking an 18-12 lead. However, Cao did not show weakness and chased closely, making it 17-18. At this point, both sides used their strengths and tied at 19 points. Then, Old Ma showed great power and won two consecutive points, thus winning the first game.

Game 2 At the beginning, both sides fought hard but gained nothing. Then, Cao's spirit seemed to wane, and Old Ma seized the opportunity to score seven points, while Cao only got one point. Old Ma then added four points, and Cao then had a chance to serve, scoring three consecutive points, making it 12-4. At this time, both sides served eight or nine times without success, making no progress. Before long, Cao's spirit suddenly revived, chasing to 11-14. But the goddess of luck still favored Old Ma, who won the final victory.

Brief Commentary on Skills The two players each have their own strengths. Old Ma is strong and powerful in his shots, while Cao is good at saving the ball. However, Cao ultimately could not defeat Old Ma because his strength was insufficient.

Wimbledon Women's Singles Semi-Finals and Quarter-Finals: British Hopes Suffer a Major Blow, Three Out of Four Eliminated 125

Mrs. Moody Remains Undefeated ｜ Jacobs Defeats Strong German Opponent

London, 27th - The Wimbledon tennis tournament continued today. The weather was hot, and 15,000 spectators crowded around the center court to watch the final eight women compete for a place in the quarter-finals.

The Last Four in the Women's Singles 126

British hopes have suffered a major blow as a result of today's competition. Three out of four players have been eliminated, and the only remaining Ms. Hillan will face Mrs. Moody in the quarter-finals, so her chances are slim. The results of today's semi-final and quarter-final matches are as follows:

(1) Ms. Hillan (England) defeated Mrs. Huddleston (England) 3-6, 6-4, 6-0

(2) Mrs. Moody (USA) defeated Ms. Round (USA) 6-0, 6-1

(3) Mrs. Mathieu (France) defeated Ms. Nutthall (England) 6-0, 6-3

(4) Ms. Jacobs (USA) defeated Mrs. Krahwinkel (Germany) 6-2, 6-4

The Tragic Situation of British Women's Defeat 127

Huddleston's Cramp Leads to Tragic Defeat In the match between Hillan and Mrs. Huddleston, Huddleston had already won the first set and was leading 4-3 in the second set. Suddenly, she suffered a cramp, so she couldn't resist, losing nine consecutive games.

Nutthall's French Stroke Errors Mrs. Mathieu vs. Nutthall's match was over in just half an hour. In the four minutes after the match, Mrs. Mathieu won four games. Nutthall's strokes were completely wrong, the baseline shots often went out of bounds, suicide touches on the net, the serve was repeated mistakes, and so on. Mrs. Mathieu had almost no opponent.

Jacobs' Triumphant Work Jacobs defeated Mrs. Krahwinkel. Jacobs' performance was top-notch. Krahwinkel was the finalist last year. In the French Open, she had a fierce battle with Mrs. Moody. Today, Helen actually defeated her.

Records of Knocking on the Bell in the Ancient Temple (37) 129

—斋夫 Do Not Remove the Garden Grass

41 Why didn't Mr. Zhu pass the old age? This was an unexpected piece of news. At first, I only thought that Old

Old Xu was spreading rumors, and I didn't believe it. What kind of material can I expect from Mr. Zhu, who actually admits that he is not a Korean, but instead makes me confused. In my opinion, Mr. Zhu will never go against the list. I thought about it again and again, but I couldn't figure it out, so I honestly asked Mr. Zhu.

Mr. Zhu said: "When I was young, I heard a saying, called: "A mouse gets into a cow's horn." You know that a cow's horn has a big opening and gets smaller and smaller as you go in, until it can't get smaller until you reach the tip of the horn. The more you drill the cow's horn, the less you can get out. In the end, there is only a dead end. A mouse getting into a cow's horn is a small shadow of traditional Chinese education. Thousands of students are drilling towards this cow's horn. Behind the students are teachers, behind the teachers are supervisors, behind the supervisors are directors, and the heads of the department and ministers are holding whips and driving groups of people into the cow's horn. The instructors desperately drive the students so they have to desperately drill. The one who drives the most vigorously is promoted to officialdom. The one who drills the most vigorously gets 100 points, and gets the most excellent diploma. I am just wandering at the entrance of the horn and don't want to go in. Even if someone is driving me from behind, I am not willing to drill. After drilling a few steps, I turn back. Shouldn't I go against the list? Why did Xu ever spread rumors? I only hate that at that time I was unwilling to drill into the cow's horn, so why not happily run to the vast sky? What can I miss about the cow's horn? Today, because of this difference in thought, this trace is left behind. It was also because I didn't have the determination to cut the nail and cut the iron at that time, that this mess was made."

So that's the way it is. My stuffy gourd has been completely broken.

Summer Silkworm Rearing in Yuhang Declines Sharply 140

Only two or three tenths of previous years

Cold weather further damages cocoons

Farmers in various cities and towns of Yuhang have recently paid attention to raising summer silkworms. However, due to the unusually poor spring cocoon harvest this year, silkworm eggs are not cheap, and cocoon prices are extremely low. Silkworm raisers have suffered great losses. Therefore, they are very discouraged about summer silkworms. Only families with mulberry leaves raise a little. The rearing of silkworms is only two or three tenths of previous years. After collecting the silkworm eggs, the weather was warm, and the silkworm eggs developed well. Early batches have abundant leaves, and late batches have also begun their first molt. Unexpectedly, the heavy rain two days ago brought severe cold, causing the silkworm eggs to shrink and delay their growth. Some have died. It is said that the future silkworm harvest will again be disappointing.

New Statistics on Qihong Tea Production 143

Qimen black tea is the highest grade tea among domestic foreign firms. The quality of its leaves and the fragrance are unparalleled in the world. Those in Europe and America who value and enjoy tea highly value Qimen tea. Therefore, market prices have gradually increased in recent years. This year, due to extremely poor weather, poor production, and harvest shortfalls, combined with low selling prices, it can be said that this is the most precarious year for Qihong tea in more than a decade. According to Qimen tea merchants, the poor tea quality this year is due to excessive rain and little sunshine from the beginning to the end of the harvesting and processing. The tea leaves were light, thin, and not supple due to water, and the green tea was not exposed to sunlight for drying, so the fragrance was naturally not good. Moreover, the processing and drying were greatly lacking. Every dan of tea leaves yielded only three and a half times its weight in dry tea. This rate is rare. It is estimated that the total number of boxed tea produced by all tea houses in the county is no more than 40,000 boxes, a decrease of more than 30,000 boxes compared to last year. The unfavorable prices for Qihong tea this year are also due to the inferior quality of the tea itself. Fortunately, the number of boxes is not large, and all tea houses have closed their operations. All boxed tea has been shipped to Shanghai. Because the Shanghai warehouses have stopped processing stem tea for a year, the production volume is even scarcer. If foreign merchants have a strong demand, the new goods arriving in Shanghai will soon be cleared.

With ocean wheat quoted down by 0.01-0.02 yuan and favorable weather prospects, flour factories, due to a decline in actual sales and difficulties in selling inventories, continued to dump futures flour despite lowering prices, as sales in the north could not proceed on a large scale. The market trend was thus extremely weak. Given this situation, the 0.08 yuan level may have to be broken. As a result, July futures fell by 0.0125 yuan compared to the previous day, August and September futures each fell by 0.01 yuan, and October and November futures each fell by 0.005 yuan.

Wheat Futures: Morning Weakness, Afternoon Rebound 147

Yesterday's wheat futures market showed a downward trend in all months after the opening in the morning. Ocean wheat quotations continued to decrease by 0.01-0.02 yuan, and the favorable weather caused significant pessimism. July futures fell to a minimum of 0.014 yuan, and August futures fell to 0.024 yuan, a drop of 0.04 yuan compared to the previous day. Distant months also fell by 0.01 yuan. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, due to a large number of short positions urgently needing to be covered and traders intending to buy, both near and distant months recovered by 0.02-0.03 yuan compared to the morning. As a result, July futures fell by 0.01 yuan, August futures were unchanged, September futures rose by 0.01 yuan, October futures were unchanged, and November futures fell by 0.03 yuan. The spot wheat market was stable. Factories selectively purchased at higher prices. Although the volume was not large, the market was very active. Kaihengjing wheat was priced at 2.93 yuan, Shuangfeng wheat at 2.92, 2.90 yuan, Taicang wheat at 2.875-2.885 yuan, Huangdu wheat at 2.85 yuan, and Anting wheat at 2.85 yuan. Waigang wheat was priced at 2.80 yuan and Shisong wheat at 2.80 yuan. A total of 2,000 bags were traded by Shen Da Fumaoxin.
